          jQuery(function($){
 	$('li.gamelist-widget-tabs').click(function(){
 		var filter = $(this).attr('gamelist-filter');
 		$(this).siblings().removeClass('active');

        jQuery(function($){
         $.getJSON('/boards/activityrss.php?limit=5',function(json){
                 var div_class = "";
                 for(var i = 0; i<json.posts.length; i++){
                         if(i==4){
                                 div_class = "last";
                         }
                         var item = json.posts[i];
                         var html = '<li class="'+div_class+'">' +
 					'<h4><a href="'+item.url+'">'+item.title+'</a></h4>' +
 					'<p>'+item.pagetext+'</p>'
                                         '</li>';
                         $(html).appendTo(".forum-hotbox");
                 }
         });
 });
